                   <path d="m16 5-1.42 1.42-1.59-1.59V16h-1.98V4.83L9.42 6.42 8 5l4-4zm4 5v11c0 1.1-.9 2-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V10c0-1.11.89-2 2-2h3v2H6v11h12V10h-3V8h3a2 2 0 0 1 2 2">

                 </div>

                </div>
               </div>
              </span>
              <span class="mweb-share-dialog yf-15uzx9j">
               <button aria-label="Share links" class="icon2-btn fin-size-medium rounded yf-r7dg9i" data-icon-type="ios-share" data-testid="mobile-share-button" data-yga='{"yLinkElement":"share","yModuleName":"consolidated-share-popup","yDestinationContentUUID":"63330001-a50d-3907-8f10-d8fd6ee49c68","yLinkText":"share-menu-open"}' data-ylk="elm:share;itc:1;sec:consolidated-share-popup;g:63330001-a50d-3907-8f10-d8fd6ee49c68;slk:share-menu-open" title="Share links">

           <div class="body-wrap yf-1muc6rc">
            <div class="body yf-v6n2s3" data-testid="article-body">
             <div class="bodyItems-wrapper">
              <figure class="yf-750ceo" data-testid="article-figure-image">
               <div class="image-container yf-lglytj" style="--max-height: 533px;">
                <div class="image-wrapper yf-lglytj" style="--aspect-ratio: 800 / 533; --img-max-width: 800px;">
                 <img alt="Keppel" class="yf-lglytj loaded" height="533" loading="eager" src="https://s.yimg.com/ny/api/res/1.2/CGDhc8AVBaNjzn9NL2HN4w--/YXBwaWQ9aGlnaGxhbmRlcjt3PTk2MDtoPTY0MDtjZj13ZWJw/https://media.zenfs.com/en/the_smart_investor_443/889afa90c85c868cef97b88dc2d90676" width="800"/>
                </div>
               </div>
               <figcaption class="yf-750ceo">
                <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
                Keppel
                <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
               </figcaption>
              </figure>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               Inflation rarely announces itself.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               It tends to rear its ugly head through the cost of everyday items and in bills that slowly start to rise, eating into our savings and fixed income investments.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               And that’s why investors turn to stocks that pay dividends during market uncertainty.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               However, not all such stocks are created equal.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <div class="wrapper yf-eondll" data-testid="inarticle-ad">
               <div class="sdaContainer dv-all sda-INARTICLE-63330001-a50d-3907-8f10-d8fd6ee49c68-1 yf-d5hqm1 overflow margin visible placeholder" data-ad-loc="mid_center" data-ad-region="main-dynamic" data-ad-size="970x250,728x90,970x90,300x250,fluid" data-ad-unit="/22888152279/sg/yfin/ros/dt/sg_yfin_ros_dt_mid_center" data-testid="ad-container" id="sda-INARTICLE-63330001-a50d-3907-8f10-d8fd6ee49c68-1" style="--placeholder-height: 250px;">
               </div>
              </div>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               Some offer far more resilience over the course of time.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               Here are the three dividend stocks that stand out when inflation starts to take a toll on our finances.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <h2 class="header-scroll yf-1u6g9f6" id="">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               <strong>
                Why Dividend Stocks Can Help During Inflation
               </strong>
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </h2>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               <a class="link" data-yga='{"yLinkElement":"context_link","yModuleName":"content-canvas","yLinkText":"Dividend investing"}' data-ylk="slk:Dividend investing;elm:context_link;itc:0;sec:content-canvas" href="https://thesmartinvestor.com.sg/the-joy-of-dividend-investing/" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">
                Dividend investing
               </a>
               can provide steady income and help cushion against market downturns.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               Strong businesses with high pricing power can raise prices and protect their margins, supporting consistent, reliable dividend payments across various market cycles.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               Growing payouts serve as an effective mechanism to offset rising living costs by increasing income streams that can outpace inflation.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <h2 class="header-scroll yf-1u6g9f6" id="">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               <strong>
                What I Look for When Inflation Is Rising
               </strong>
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </h2>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               Top investors look for a combination of pricing power and essential demand to protect portfolios and maintain profit margins.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               Focusing on strong and consistent free cash flow is a reliable indicator, as it identifies companies that generate real cash, rather than just accounting profits.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               Dividend sustainability and growth potential are the bread and butter of a robust investment strategy.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <div class="wrapper yf-eondll" data-testid="inarticle-ad">
               <div class="sdaContainer dv-all sda-INARTICLE-63330001-a50d-3907-8f10-d8fd6ee49c68-2 yf-d5hqm1 overflow margin visible placeholder" data-ad-loc="mid_center_2" data-ad-region="main-dynamic" data-ad-size="970x250,728x90,970x90,300x250" data-ad-unit="/22888152279/sg/yfin/ros/dt/sg_yfin_ros_dt_mid_center" data-testid="ad-container" id="sda-INARTICLE-63330001-a50d-3907-8f10-d8fd6ee49c68-2" style="--placeholder-height: 250px;">
               </div>
              </div>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               This is because companies with low debt and a track record of consistent dividend increases tend to outperform over time, as their payouts are better supported through changing market conditions.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <h2 class="header-scroll yf-1u6g9f6" id="">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               <strong>
                Keppel Ltd. (SGX: BN4) — The Pricing Power Leader
               </strong>
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </h2>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               <a class="link" data-yga='{"yLinkElement":"context_link","yModuleName":"content-canvas","yLinkText":"Keppel"}' data-ylk="slk:Keppel;elm:context_link;itc:0;sec:content-canvas" href="https://thesmartinvestor.com.sg/oil-price-above-us100-should-you-buy-keppel-stock-now/" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">
                Keppel
               </a>
               , a leading Singapore blue-chip company, runs a tight ship as a global asset manager with a clear focus on growing its income from infrastructure, real assets, and fund management.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               Most of its projects rely on long-term contracts or regulated pricing, which helps keep margins steady even when costs rise.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               While revenue edged up 3.4% year on year (YoY) to S$5.98 billion  in FY2025, the group delivered much stronger profit growth from its core businesses.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               Keppel’s continuing operations lifted net profit by 39% YoY to S$1.1 billion.
               <br/>
               <br/>
               This divergence between profit and revenue points to improving profitability, driven by stronger pricing discipline and higher-value income streams.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               Keppel also ramped up its total dividend to S$0.47 per share – 38% higher than last year.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               At the current share price of S$11.88, that works out to a yield of about 4%.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               This highlights how pricing power and being a broad-based market leader is one of the strongest defences against inflation.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
             </div>
             <div class="readmore yf-11souuj">
              <button aria-label="Story continues" class="secondary-btn fin-size-large readmore-button rounded yf-r7dg9i" data-yga='{"yLinkElement":"readmore","yModuleName":"content-canvas","yLinkText":"Story continues"}' data-ylk="elm:readmore;itc:1;sec:content-canvas;slk:Story%20continues" title="Story continues">
               <span>
                Story continues
               </span>
              </button>
             </div>
             <div class="read-more-wrapper" data-testid="read-more" style="display: none">
              <h2 class="header-scroll yf-1u6g9f6" id="">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               <strong>
                OCBC Bank (SGX: O39) — The Dividend Growth Compounder
               </strong>
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </h2>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               OCBC’s dividend growth has been both consistent and accelerating in recent years.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               In the past five years, total dividends almost doubled, moving from S$0.53 to about S$0.99, driven by solid earnings and careful capital management.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               Ignoring special payouts, ordinary dividends still climbed from S$0.53 per share in 2021 to S$0.83 per share in 2025, a clear sign the trend is heading upward.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <div class="wrapper yf-eondll" data-testid="inarticle-ad">
               <div class="sdaContainer dv-all sda-INARTICLE-63330001-a50d-3907-8f10-d8fd6ee49c68-3 yf-d5hqm1 overflow margin visible placeholder" data-ad-loc="mid_center_3" data-ad-region="main-dynamic" data-ad-size="970x250,728x90,970x90,300x250" data-ad-unit="/22888152279/sg/yfin/ros/dt/sg_yfin_ros_dt_mid_center" data-testid="ad-container" id="sda-INARTICLE-63330001-a50d-3907-8f10-d8fd6ee49c68-3" style="--placeholder-height: 250px;">
               </div>
              </div>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               With its FY2025 dividend at S$0.99 per share and the current share price sitting around S$22.72, OCBC’s yield stands at 4.4%.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               <a class="link" data-yga='{"yLinkElement":"context_link","yModuleName":"content-canvas","yLinkText":"OCBC"}' data-ylk="slk:OCBC;elm:context_link;itc:0;sec:content-canvas" href="https://thesmartinvestor.com.sg/bought-ocbcs-shares-10-years-ago-heres-how-much-you-will-have-now/" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">
                OCBC
               </a>
               hit a big milestone on 1 April 2026, joining DBS in a rare group of Singapore companies with a market capitalisation above S$100 billion.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               Backed by its latest financial results for FY2025, showing net profit of S$7.42 billion and record total income of S$14.6 billion, OCBC is in a strong position to keep rewarding investors.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <h2 class="header-scroll yf-1u6g9f6" id="">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               <strong>
                Mapletree Industrial Trust (SGX: ME8U), or MIT — The High-Quality Income Anchor
               </strong>
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </h2>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               <a class="link" data-yga='{"yLinkElement":"context_link","yModuleName":"content-canvas","yLinkText":"MIT"}' data-ylk="slk:MIT;elm:context_link;itc:0;sec:content-canvas" href="https://thesmartinvestor.com.sg/better-buy-mapletree-logistics-trust-vs-mapletree-industrial-trust-3/" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">
                MIT
               </a>
               stands out as a steady income anchor due to its diversified portfolio – covering everything from data centres and business parks to high-tech buildings.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               Besides some short-term bumps, mostly from currency swings and lease renewals, its Singapore assets keep pulling their weight.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               Occupancies remain strong, and rents keep trending up, which helps keep investors at ease.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               Its latest quarterly results (3QFY2025/26) back this up. MIT delivered a distribution per unit (DPU) of S$0.0317 – a slight dip of 0.3% from the quarter before.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <div class="wrapper yf-eondll" data-testid="inarticle-ad">
               <div class="sdaContainer dv-all sda-INARTICLE-63330001-a50d-3907-8f10-d8fd6ee49c68-4 yf-d5hqm1 overflow margin visible placeholder" data-ad-loc="mid_center_4" data-ad-region="main-dynamic" data-ad-size="970x250,728x90,970x90,300x250" data-ad-unit="/22888152279/sg/yfin/ros/dt/sg_yfin_ros_dt_mid_center" data-testid="ad-container" id="sda-INARTICLE-63330001-a50d-3907-8f10-d8fd6ee49c68-4" style="--placeholder-height: 250px;">
               </div>
              </div>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               Nonetheless, distributions have stayed stable over the years, typically landing between S$0.12 and S$0.14 per unit.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               With a unit price of S$2.07 and an annualised DPU of S$0.13, its yield sits at 6.3%.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               That puts MIT near the top for dependable income for S-REITs.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               From a balance sheet perspective, MIT stays solid.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               Leverage sits at 37.2%, with an interest coverage ratio of 3.9 times as of 31 December 2025.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               Even as borrowing costs go up, it has kept plenty of financial wiggle room.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               Bottom line: In choppy markets, it pays to anchor your portfolio with something you can trust.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <h2 class="header-scroll yf-1u6g9f6" id="">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               <strong>
                What I Would Avoid
               </strong>
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </h2>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               Avoiding
               <a class="link" data-yga='{"yLinkElement":"context_link","yModuleName":"content-canvas","yLinkText":"high-yield stocks"}' data-ylk="slk:high-yield stocks;elm:context_link;itc:0;sec:content-canvas" href="https://thesmartinvestor.com.sg/3-mistakes-singapore-investors-make-when-chasing-high-yields/" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">
                high-yield stocks
               </a>
               with weak cash flow is an essential strategy for protecting capital.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               These are “dividend traps”, or companies with high yields driven by falling share prices, which often lead to dividend cuts.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               It also pays to steer clear of companies that rely heavily on debt.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               In a rising rate and inflationary environment, leverage can quickly become a burden, increasing both risk and portfolio volatility.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <div class="wrapper yf-eondll" data-testid="inarticle-ad">
               <div class="sdaContainer dv-all sda-INARTICLE-63330001-a50d-3907-8f10-d8fd6ee49c68-5 yf-d5hqm1 overflow margin visible placeholder" data-ad-loc="mid_center_5" data-ad-region="main-dynamic" data-ad-size="970x250,728x90,970x90,300x250" data-ad-unit="/22888152279/sg/yfin/ros/dt/sg_yfin_ros_dt_mid_center" data-testid="ad-container" id="sda-INARTICLE-63330001-a50d-3907-8f10-d8fd6ee49c68-5" style="--placeholder-height: 250px;">
               </div>
              </div>
              <h2 class="header-scroll yf-1u6g9f6" id="">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               <strong>
                Get Smart: Inflation Rewards the Right Kind of Income
               </strong>
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </h2>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               When inflation strikes, we need to repeat this: Not every dividend stock gives the same protection.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               It’s not just about how much you earn, but whether your income can keep up as prices rise.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               The strongest dividend stocks are those that pair solid fundamentals with the ability to steadily grow their payouts over time.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               It’s not just your imagination – filling up the tank is hitting the wallet harder than it has in years. With oil prices whipsawing and the NASDAQ behaving like a roller coaster, “paralysis by analysis” is a real risk for investors right now.

                Secure your seat
               </a>
               at our upcoming free webinar to see how we manage cash and pick winners while the headlines are screaming “Correction.”
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
              <p class="yf-1fy9kyt">
               <!-- HTML_TAG_START -->
               The headlines feel worse than the market itself.
               <!-- HTML_TAG_END -->
              </p>
